Active Hero's Echo
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby players.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: + 4%, Duration: 40 min


Active Elemental Slash
Master Level 1
Description Attack enemies in front of you with pure, primal energy.
Level 1 MP Cost: 0, Damage: 130%, Number of Attacks: 1, Max Enemies Hit: 3


Active Imperial Recall
Master Level 1
Description Return to the Empress using Shinsoo's power.
Level 1 MP Cost: 100, return to Ereve immediately.
Cooldown: 600 sec.


Passive Elemental Harmony
Master Level 1
Description Use the harmony of nature to build affinity for an element of your choosing.
Level 1 Luck increases 1 for every 2 levels the character gains


Passive Elemental Expert
Master Level 1
Description Become an expert of the elements to increase Attack Power and Magic ATT.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +10%


Passive Elemental Shift
Master Level 1
Description Jump in any direction except down by pressing a direction key and jump in midair.
Level 1 MP Cost: 4, jumps further in the appropriate direction

Passive Cygnus Blessing (Thief)
Master Level 10
Description Blessings from an awakened Empress Cygnus protect you from harm.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 5 times, once for each unique Cygnus Knights job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +7, Abnormal Status Resistance: +1, All Elemental Resistance: +1%
10 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +25, Abnormal Status Resistance: +15, All Elemental Resistance: +15%

Active Dark Elemental
Master Level 10
Description Summons a dark element to gain its power.
This skill can be toggled on/off by using the skill key.
Level 10 required to learn Adaptive Darkness.
Level 1 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 53% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 1% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
10 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 80% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 4% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
Active Dark Elemental
Master Level 10
Description Summons a dark element to gain its power.
This skill can be toggled on/off by using the skill key.
Level 10 required to learn Adaptive Darkness.
Level 1 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 53% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 1% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
2 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 56% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 1% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
3 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 59% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 1% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
4 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 62% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 2% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
5 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 65% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 2% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
6 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 68% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 2% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
7 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 71% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 3% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
8 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 74% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 3% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
9 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 77% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 3% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.
10 Hit enemies with Throwing Stars Skill for a 20% chance to create a Mark of Darkness that stacks 2 times. Marked enemies will take 80% damage over time per stack every second for 5 seconds, and if Night Walkers attack these enemies, they'll ignore 4% defense per stacked Mark of Darkness.

Active Shadow Bat
Master Level 20
Description Summons a Shadow Bat, which occasionally attacks when you do. Its attack rate is doubled against enemies marked with Darkness, and as many summoned bats attack as there are marks. 1 additional Shadow Bat is created at this time.
This skill is unaffected by enemy attack reflection skills. Cannot be used at the same time as Ravenous Bat. It's a dark-attribute attack.
This skill can be toggled on/off by using the skill key.
Required Skill: Dark Elemental Lv. 1
Level 20 required to learn Bat Affinity.
Level 1 Summons a Shadow Bat for 60 sec for every 3 times that you hit with a Throwing Star skill. Max number of bats: 2.
When using a Throwing Star skill, there is a 50% chance for it to fly towards the target and inflict 112% damage, then bounce off 3 enemies and inflict the same amount of damage before disappearing. Damage Against Normal Enemies: +35%
Recovers 1% of Max HP on first damage.
20 Summons a Shadow Bat for 60 sec for every 3 times that you hit with a Throwing Star skill. Max number of bats: 2.
When using a Throwing Star skill, there is a 50% chance for it to fly towards the target and inflict 150% damage, then bounce off 3 enemies and inflict the same amount of damage before disappearing. Damage Against Normal Enemies: +35%
Recovers 1% of Max HP on first damage.

Active Shadow Jump
Master Level 1
Description Use while in the middle of a jump to jump twice in a row. Can also be used with the Jump Key. Also, the last attack of throwing skills can be canceled with the Jump Key. If you've learned Dark Sight and used the Jump Key during the last attack of a throwing skill, Dark Sight will be activated automatically for a short time.
With Action Customization enabled, hold the right or left arrow key while pressing the skill key to jump in the corresponding direction, otherwise you will jump in place.
SP is not required for this skill, and it can be used upon job advancing to Night Walker.
Action Customization On/Off: Right-click
Level 1 MP Cost: 5. Allows you to jump a greater distance.
Using the Jump Key during throwing skills will cause you to enter Dark Sight state for 2 sec.
If you dodge an attack that deals damage proportional to Max HP while the triggered Dark Sight is active, its remaining duration will be reduced by 20% of the full duration.
Show/hide all levels
Active Dark Sight
Master Level 5
Description Hide in the shadows for a short time. While Dark Sight is active, you cannot be hit by enemies, but attacking will reveal you. The cooldown will change when Dark Sight is deactivated, depending on damage dodged. Using Shadow Jump does not deactivate Dark Sight. Press the skill key again to deactivate Dark Sight.
Level 1 MP Cost: 28, hides in the shadows for 40 seconds.
When Dark Sight is deactivated, cooldown increased per attack dodged: 3 seconds. Stacks up to 5 times.
5 MP Cost: 20, hides in the shadows for 200 seconds.
When Dark Sight is deactivated, cooldown increased per attack dodged: 3 seconds. Stacks up to 5 times.

Active Shadow Dodge
Master Level 1
Description Quickly move backwards.
You can move in the air and during the last attack of throwing skills, and cannot be pushed back when moving. If you've learned Dark Sight and used it during the last attack of a throwing skill, Dark Sight will be activated automatically for a short time.
SP is not required for this skill, and it can be used upon job advancing to Night Walker.
Level 1 MP Cost: 7. Allows you to move a certain distance backwards.
Using during throwing skills will cause you to enter Dark Sight state for 2 sec.
If you dodge an attack that deals damage proportional to Max HP while the triggered Dark Sight is active, its remaining duration will be reduced by 20% of the full duration.

Active Triple Throw
Master Level 15
Description [Throw]
Throws 3 Throwing Stars in a row at the target. The last attack uses the power of Darkness to deal greater dark-attribute damage. The throwing stars attack the boss with the highest HP first.
Level 1 MP Cost: 17, Throwing Stars Cost: 3, Damage: 168% 2 times, Damage: 336% 1 time
15 MP Cost: 20, Throwing Stars Cost: 3, Damage: 210% 2 times, Damage: 420% 1 time

Active Dark Servant
Master Level 20
Description Summons a shadow which copies your actions after a short delay. The copied actions are limited to throwing stars and movement skills. Your shadow disappears when the summon time runs out. All attacks of the shadow are dark-attribute and can activate Marks of Darkness, Shadow Bats, or Ravenous Bats without being affected by attack reflection.
Level 20 required to learn Shadow Illusion.
Level 1 MP Cost: 46, Summon Duration: 85 sec. Your shadow attacks, dealing 51% of the Final Damage of your throwing star skills.
20 MP Cost: 65, Summon Duration: 180 sec. Your shadow attacks, dealing 70% of the Final Damage of your throwing star skills.

Active Darkness Ascending
Master Level 5
Description When hit by a fatal attack, the power of darkness will restore you back to life.
Not affected by Cooldown reset.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 1 MP Cost: 190. When hit by an attack that would prove fatal, consume the buff and recover 10% of Max HP per 3 sec. If Shadow Bats and Ravenous Bats are currently summoned, they are consumed to recover 6% extra HP per bat.
Invincible for 2 sec while recovering, and again at the end of skill.
Upon consuming buff - Cooldown: 1800 sec
5 MP Cost: 150. When hit by an attack that would prove fatal, consume the buff and recover 50% of Max HP per 3 sec. If Shadow Bats and Ravenous Bats are currently summoned, they are consumed to recover 10% extra HP per bat.
Invincible for 2 sec while recovering, and again at the end of skill.
Upon consuming buff - Cooldown: 1800 sec

Passive Shadow Momentum
Master Level 20
Description Gives the attack inertia to use throwing skills even faster, and increases Final Damage permanently. Obtain inertia by moving a certain distance, and the last attack can be canceled when using throwing skills consecutively. The higher the inertia level, the faster you can cancel. This buff is not affected by buff duration extension effects.
Right-click to lock activation effect.
Level 1 Move a certain distance to obtain inertia for 11 sec, stacks up to Lv. 3.
Permanently increases Final Damage by 10%
20 Move a certain distance to obtain inertia for 30 sec, stacks up to Lv. 3.
Permanently increases Final Damage by 20%

Passive Bat Affinity II
Master Level 20
Description Enhances the Shadow Bat through communion. Summons an enhanced Shadow Bat for every fixed number of bats in the place that was attacked to deal explosion damage. The enhanced Shadow Bat isn't enhanced by Bat Affinity and Bat Affinity II, and is unaffected by attack reflection. All attacks of the enhanced Shadow Bat are dark-attribute attacks.
Required Skill: Bat Affinity Lv. 20
Level 20 required to learn Bat Affinity III
Level 1 Shadow Bat's Max Summon Limit: 1, Damage: +55% points, Number of Bounces: +1
Summons enhanced Shadow Bat for every 5 Shadow Bats summoned.
Enhanced Shadow Bat: 100% chance to fly towards target when using a Throwing Star skill to inflict 325% damage, then bounce off 6 enemies and inflict the same amount of damage before disappearing. Creates an explosion for every attack that deals 102% damage 3 times up to 3 enemies nearby.
If a single enemy receives several explosions, Final Damage is decreased by 50% starting with the second explosion.
Enhanced Shadow Bat Damage Against Normal Enemies: +35%
20 Shadow Bat's Max Summon Limit: 1, Damage: +150% points, Number of Bounces: +1
Summons enhanced Shadow Bat for every 5 Shadow Bats summoned.
Enhanced Shadow Bat: 100% chance to fly towards target when using a Throwing Star skill to inflict 420% damage, then bounce off 6 enemies and inflict the same amount of damage before disappearing. Creates an explosion for every attack that deals 140% damage 3 times up to 3 enemies nearby.

Active Shadow Stitch
Master Level 20
Description Detonates condensed shadows to lock nearby enemies. Increases incapacitation in proportion to the condensed duration. Cannot be pushed back when condensing shadows. Unaffected by attack reflection. It's a dark-attribute attack.
Level 1 MP Cost: 54, Condense surrounding shadows by holding the key up to 5 sec.
Releasing will detonate the condensed shadows. Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 470%, Number of Attacks: 3. Attacked enemies are incapacitated for 10 sec. Incapacitation increases by 1 sec, up to 12 sec, for every 0.5 sec of the condensed duration
Incapacitation increases up to 100% depending on damage inflicted with Shadow Stitch
Cooldown: 180 sec

Active Ravenous Bat
Master Level 20
Description Summons a Ravenous Bat thirsting for more blood, which occasionally attacks when you do. As many summoned bats attack as there are enemies marked with Darkness. 1 additional Ravenous Bat is created at this time. It targets the boss with the highest HP first and is unaffected by attack reflection. Cannot be used at the same time as Shadow Bat. It's a dark-attribute attack.
This skill can be toggled on/off by using the skill key.
Required Skill: Dark Elemental Lv. 1
Level 1 Summons a Ravenous Bat for 60 sec for every 3 times that you hit with a Throwing Star skill. Max number of bats: 5.
When using a Throwing Star skill, there is a 100% chance to fly towards the target and inflict 385% damage 2 times. Recovers 1% of Max HP upon hitting.
20 Summons a Ravenous Bat for 60 sec for every 3 times that you hit with a Throwing Star skill. Max number of bats: 5.
When using a Throwing Star skill, there is a 100% chance to fly towards the target and inflict 480% damage 2 times. Recovers 1% of Max HP upon hitting.
21 Summons a Ravenous Bat for 60 sec for every 3 times that you hit with a Throwing Star skill. Max number of bats: 5.
When using a Throwing Star skill, there is a 100% chance to fly towards the target and inflict 485% damage 2 times. Recovers 1% of Max HP upon hitting.
22 Summons a Ravenous Bat for 60 sec for every 3 times that you hit with a Throwing Star skill. Max number of bats: 5.
When using a Throwing Star skill, there is a 100% chance to fly towards the target and inflict 490% damage 2 times. Recovers 1% of Max HP upon hitting.

Passive Bat Affinity III
Master Level 30
Description Enhances the Shadow Bat through communion. Summons an enhanced Ravenous Bat for every fixed number of Ravenous Bats that deals more powerful damage. The enhanced Ravenous Bat isn't enhanced by Bat Affinity, Bat Affinity II, and Bat Affinity III, and targets the boss with the highest HP first. Enhanced Ravenous Bat is a dark-attribute attack unaffected by attack reflection.
Required Skill: Bat Affinity II Lv. 20
Level 30 required to learn Shadow Bite
Level 1 Shadow Bat's Attack Chance: 30%, Max Summon Limit: 1, Damage: +84% points, Number of Bounces: +1
Enhanced Shadow Bat Damage: +84% points, Explosion Damage: +45% points
Shadow Bat Damage Against Normal Enemies: +50%
Summons enhanced Ravenous Bat for every 5 Ravenous Bats summoned.
Enhanced Ravenous Bat: 100% chance to fly towards target when using a Throwing Star skill to inflict 335% damage 3 times, recovers 5% of Max HP upon hitting

Master Level 15
Description Absorbs liveliness from your enemies to create a protective shield for yourself while you set your Mark of Darkness. Protective Shield will not be affected by buff duration increase.

Active Shadow Illusion
Level Requirement 140
Master Level 1
Description Summons 3 shadows that copy your actions after a short delay. The copied actions are limited to throwing stars and movement skills. Your shadows disappear when the summon time runs out. All attacks of the shadows are dark-attribute and can activate Marks of Darkness, Shadow Bats, or Ravenous Bats without being affected by attack reflection. Required Skill: Dark Servant Lv. 20
Level 1 MP Cost: 200, Summon Duration: 30 sec, Your shadow attacks, dealing 70%, 50%, and 30% of the Final Damage of your throwing skills.
Cooldown: 180 sec

Active Erda Nova
Master Level 25
Description Collect Erda from within yourself and from the surrounding area, then detonate it around your enemies. The Erda of attacked enemies will become disrupted, which will bind their movements. Can deal damage to enemies even when they are under Attack Ignore. Also ignores Attack Reflection.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 156%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 216 sec.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy
Cooldown: 40 sec
Erda Fountain
Object Summon Duration: 60 sec. Every time enemies in a map with the summoned object are defeated, the Erda released from the enemies condenses around the object.
Defeating 12 or more will release the gathered Erda, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 4
Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +1]
25 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 55 sec, restores 30% HP when used, able to use 17 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 65 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +5]
30 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 60 sec, restores 35% HP when used, able to use 20 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 60 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +6]

Active Phalanx Charge
Master Level 25
Description Summons brave Spearmen of the Cygnus Knights to charge enemies in a phalanx formation. The spearmen slow down upon touching an enemy. Press the skill key again to change their direction of movement. Unaffected by attack reflection and can be resisted by some monsters.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 41
Spearmen disappear when the number of attacks is reached, they move a certain distance, or after a certain duration. Activate the skill again to change their direction.
Cooldown: 30 sec

Active Venom Burst
Master Level 25
Description Causes the poison inflicting nearby enemies to burst and spread.
Level 1 MP Cost: 300. Consumes all active Damage-Over-Time stacks on up to 12 poisoned enemies in range, and instantly inflicts 100% of their remaining damage, plus an additional 520% damage 6 times.
Additional damage is +15% per remaining second of consumed DoT stacks, up to 5
Afterwards, spreads the original DoT damage across up to 10 nearby enemies
Cooldown: 8 sec.
[Passive Effects - Bonus DoT Chance: 50% to deal 166% damage every 1 sec. for 8 sec.]
25 MP Cost: 300. Consumes all active Damage-Over-Time stacks on up to 12 poisoned enemies in range, and instantly inflicts 100% of their remaining damage, plus an additional 1000% damage 6 times.
Additional damage is +15% per remaining second of consumed DoT stacks, up to 5
Afterwards, spreads the original DoT damage across up to 10 nearby enemies
Cooldown: 8 sec.
[Passive Effects - Bonus DoT Chance: 50% to deal 310% damage every 1 sec. for 8 sec.]

Afterwards, spreads the original DoT damage across up to 10 nearby enemies
Cooldown: 8 sec.

Active Last Resort
Master Level 25
Description You vow to destroy your enemies at any cost. You can renew your vow to empower its effects by using the skill again while it's active. Using the skill with the down arrow key will immediately renew your vow. With Action Customization enabled, you can renew your vow by pressing its key again, without use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 10% of Max HP, reduces Avoidability (including Bonus Evasion) and increases Final Damage for 30 sec, Hit Damage increased if attacked within a certain percentage of your max HP.
Enters 2nd Stage with remaining duration being reduced to 50% when skill is used again during 1st Stage, skill ends when used again during 2nd Stage.
1st Stage - Avoidability: -20%, Hit Damage: +10%, Final Damage: +10%
2nd Stage - Avoidability: -90%, Hit Damage: +30%, Final Damage: +24%
Cooldown: 90 sec

Class-Specific Skills

Show/hide all levels
Active Shadow Spear
Master Level 25
Description The shadows on the ground coalesce to form a spear that pierces enemies. Unaffected by attack reflection. Has no effect in towns. It's a dark-attribute attack.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, Duration: 58, shadows form on the ground every time you use a dark attribute skill (except Shadow Spear and summons).
The shadows slowly gather into a spear, dealing 183% damage 2 times on up to 8 enemies
If there are enough shadows, they'll form into a giant spear, with a 3.9 sec. cooldown, that deals 416% damage 6 times against up to 12 enemies
All the Shadow Spear's attacks increase Damage Against Normal Monsters by 25%
Cooldown: 192 sec.

Active Greater Dark Servant
Master Level 25
Description Summons an immovable shadow. The shadow faces in the direction of the boss with the highest Max HP, or in the direction of the enemy with the highest Max HP if there is no boss, and mimics throwing-star attacks. It cannot be injured, and vanishes when its duration ends.
You may activate the skill again to swap places with the shadow or use it with the down arrow key to re-summon the shadow to your current location. However, you cannot do this while in the air. A separate cooldown is applied when the shadow is called back.
All attacks of the shadows are dark-attribute and unaffected by attack reflection. Capable of triggering Mark of Darkness, Shadow Bat, and Ravenous Bat.
Level 1 MP Cost: 800, Summon Duration: 30 sec. Shadow attacks from a fixed location, dealing additional 26% of the Final Damage of your throwing star skills.
Activate to swap places up to 3 times
Shadow Re-summon Cooldown: 1.5 sec
Cooldown: 60 sec
25 MP Cost: 800, Summon Duration: 42 sec. Shadow attacks from a fixed location, dealing additional 50% of the Final Damage of your throwing star skills.
Activate to swap places up to 3 times
Shadow Re-summon Cooldown: 1.5 sec
Cooldown: 60 sec
30 MP Cost: 800, Summon Duration: 45 sec. Shadow attacks from a fixed location, dealing additional 55% of the Final Damage of your throwing star skills.
Activate to swap places up to 3 times
Shadow Re-summon Cooldown: 1.5 sec
Cooldown: 60 sec

Active Shadow Bite
Master Level 25
Description Make your enemies' shadows attack them and strip them of their power, temporarily increasing Final Damage. If Shadow Bat and Ravenous Bat can be summoned, the bats are created in the location of the enemies and immediately attack. The bats created by Shadow Bat aren't enhanced. It's a dark-attribute attack.
Required Skill: Bat Affinity III Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 1500, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 14, deals 702% damage to bosses, creates a Shadow Bat and Ravenous Bat where an enemy received an attack if a bat can be summoned.
If an enemy has been defeated by Shadow Bite, the Final Damage increases by 2% per 1 enemy for 20 sec. If you attacked a boss monster, the Final Damage increases by 8%. The Final Damage increased by Shadow Bite is applied up to 10%.
Cooldown: 15 sec
25 MP Cost: 1500, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 900%, Number of Attacks: 14, deals 1350% damage to bosses, creates a Shadow Bat and Ravenous Bat where an enemy received an attack if a bat can be summoned.
If an enemy has been defeated by Shadow Bite, the Final Damage increases by 2% per 1 enemy for 20 sec. If you attacked a boss monster, the Final Damage increases by 16%. The Final Damage increased by Shadow Bite is applied up to 18%.
Cooldown: 15 sec
30 MP Cost: 1500, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 990%, Number of Attacks: 14, deals 1485% damage to bosses, creates a Shadow Bat and Ravenous Bat where an enemy received an attack if a bat can be summoned.
If an enemy has been defeated by Shadow Bite, the Final Damage increases by 2% per 1 enemy for 20 sec. If you attacked a boss monster, the Final Damage increases by 18%. The Final Damage increased by Shadow Bite is applied up to 20%.
Cooldown: 15 sec

Active Rapid Throw
Master Level 25
Description [Throw]
Toss countless throwing stars at blinding speed. If you use this skill in the air, you'll hover while you toss them. Using Rapid Throw while Dark Sight is active does not deactivate Dark Sight. Rapid Throw is unaffected by Shadow Momentum's inertia effect. Each throwing star is applied at most once to the throwing star skill count of Shadow Bat and Ravenous Bat. It's a dark-attribute attack, but consecutive throw attacks have higher damage even though the shadow from Shadow Spear isn't formed.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, consecutively throw shadow throwing stars with 494% damage 5 times up to 8 enemies for 1.8 sec then finish with a huge shadow throwing star that attacks up to 10 enemies with 884% damage 13 times
Dark Sight for 4 sec while skill is in use. Tap repeatedly to increase the consecutive throwing duration up to 3 sec
While Shadow Spear is active, Consecutive Throw Attack Damage: +145% points
Cooldown: 90 sec

Cooldown: 90 sec

Active Sol Janus: Dawn
Master Level 30
Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.
Cyclic Rings are unaffected by attack reflection.

Active Silence
Master Level 30
Description With the power of infinite darkness, calls forth the Shadow Bat to silence enemies with fear.
For a certain period of time, when the attack hits, the Shadow Bat morphs into huge Shadow Throwing Stars, continuously targeting and attacking the enemy. The Shadow Throwing Stars trigger Dark Elemental, Shadow Bat, and Ravenous Bat effects with each attack.
The Shadow Throwing Stars target the boss with the highest max HP first. Unaffected by attack reflection.

Lv. 10: Ignore Defense +20%
Lv. 20: Boss Damage +20%
Lv. 30: Ignore Defense +30%, Boss Damage +30%
Level 1 MP Cost: 1200, invincible during casting
Chase Cuts occur 34 times which attack up to 15 enemies with 481% damage 12 times
For 30 seconds, when the attack hits, the Shadow Bat transforms into 3 huge Shadow Throwing Stars to track and attack the enemy
Shadow Throwing Stars: attack 12 times with 465% damage, after hitting the enemy, the Shadow Throwing Stars attack by bouncing up to 5 times, Shadow Throwing Stars Recreation Cooldown: 3 seconds
Cooldown: 360 seconds
30 MP Cost: 1200, invincible during casting
Chase Cuts occur 34 times which attack up to 15 enemies with 945% damage 12 times
For 30 seconds, when the attack hits, the Shadow Bat transforms into 3 huge Shadow Throwing Stars to track and attack the enemy
Shadow Throwing Stars: attack 12 times with 900% damage, after hitting the enemy, the Shadow Throwing Stars attack by bouncing up to 5 times, Shadow Throwing Stars Recreation Cooldown: 3 seconds
Cooldown: 360 seconds

Mastery Skills

Mastery Skills are affected by Hyper Skill passives (if applicable) and Boost Node enhancements applied to the base skill.

Show/hide all levels
Active HEXA Quintuple Star
Master Level 30
Description [Throw]
Throws 5 Throwing Stars in a row at the target. The last attack uses the power of Darkness to deal greater dark-attribute damage. The last attack is enhanced to Jet Black Throwing Stars at regular intervals. These throwing stars fly a longer distance, attack all enemies along the way, and deal greater dark-attribute damage.
The throwing stars prioritize attacking the boss with the highest HP first.
Required Skill: Quintuple Star Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 45, Throwing Stars Cost: 5
Damage: 272% 4 times, Damage: 1088% 1 time
Every 6 seconds, the last attack is enhanced to Jet Black Throwing Stars.
30 MP Cost: 52, Throwing Stars Cost: 5
Damage: 330% 4 times, Damage: 1320% 1 time
Every 6 seconds, the last attack is enhanced to Jet Black Throwing Stars.

Active HEXA Quintuple Star [1]
Master Level 30
Description [Throw]
Throws 5 Throwing Stars in a row at the target. The last attack is enhanced to Jet Black Throwing Stars. These throwing stars they fly a longer distance, attack all enemies along the way, and deal greater dark-attribute damage. The throwing stars prioritize attacking the boss with the highest HP first.
Required Skill: Quintuple Star Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 45, Throwing Stars Cost: 5, Damage: 272% 4 times
The final attack is enhanced Jet Black Throwing Stars that strike up to 8 enemies with 213% damage 7 times
30 MP Cost: 52, Throwing Stars Cost: 5, Damage: 330% 4 times
The final attack is enhanced Jet Black Throwing Stars that strike up to 8 enemies with 300% damage 7 times

Active HEXA Shadow Bat
Master Level 30
Description Summon a Shadow Bat, which occasionally attacks when you do. Its attack rate is doubled against enemies marked with Darkness, and as many summoned bats attack as there are marks. 1 additional Shadow Bat is created at this time.
Unaffected by attack reflection. Cannot be used at the same time as Ravenous Bat. It's a dark-attribute attack.
This skill can be toggled On/Off.
Required Skill: Ravenous Bat Lv. 20, Bat Affinity III Lv. 30
Level 1 Summon a Shadow Bat for 60 sec for every 3 times that you hit with a Throwing Star skill. Max number of bats: 2.
When using a Throwing Star skill, there is a 50% chance for it to fly towards the target and inflict 910% damage, then bounce off 3 enemies and inflict the same amount of damage before disappearing.
Normal Enemy Damage: +85%, Does not stack with Shadow Bat and Bat Affinity III.
Recovers 1% of Max HP on first damage.
30 Summon a Shadow Bat for 60 sec for every 3 times that you hit with a Throwing Star skill. Max number of bats: 2.
When using a Throwing Star skill, there is a 50% chance for it to fly towards the target and inflict 1200% damage, then bounce off 3 enemies and inflict the same amount of damage before disappearing.
Normal Enemy Damage: +85%, Does not stack with Shadow Bat and Bat Affinity III.
Recovers 1% of Max HP on first damage.

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
